      <script>
  window.lazyLoadScript = function(options) {
    var src = options.src;
    var id = options.id;
    var timeout = options.timeout || 2000;
    var onLoad = options.onLoad;
    var onError = options.onError;
    var crossOrigin = options.crossOrigin;

    if (options.delayUntilInteraction) {
      var triggered = false;
      var events = ['keydown', 'click', 'scroll', 'mousemove', 'touchstart'];

      var triggerLoad = function() {
        if (triggered) return;
        triggered = true;
        events.forEach(function(e) { window.removeEventListener(e, triggerLoad); });

        options.delayUntilInteraction = false;
        window.lazyLoadScript(options);
      };

      events.forEach(function(e) {
        window.addEventListener(e, triggerLoad, { passive: true, once: true });
      });

      return;
    }

    function loadScript() {
      if (id && document.getElementById(id)) return;
      if (!id && document.querySelector('script[src="' + src + '"]')) return;

      var script = document.createElement('script');
      script.type = 'text/javascript';
      script.async = true;
      script.src = src;
      if (id) script.id = id;
      if (crossOrigin) script.crossOrigin = crossOrigin;

      if (onLoad) {
        script.onload = function() {
          try { onLoad(); } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
        };
      }

      if (onError) {
        script.onerror = function() {
          try { onError(); } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
        };
      }

      document.head.appendChild(script);
    }

    if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) {
      requestIdleCallback(loadScript, { timeout: timeout });
    } else {
      setTimeout(loadScript, 34);
    }
  };
</script>

It is a major player in the private ownership sector as well as the charter sector. Its models offer versatility, comfort, stability, and performance in equal measure.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eToday, Lagoon is a brand of Groupe Beneteau, which purchased the company in 1995. The company itself dates back to 1984, and built the first Lagoon 55 in 1987. By 1994 that lineup expanded to include five more models\u0026mdash;all built to match the high standards of race boats\u0026mdash;constructed in epoxy, glass, carbon and Kevlar. In 1997, the Lagoon 410 became its first production volume catamaran\u0026mdash;a model remembered for its iconic and innovative vertical windows. The Lagoon 380, a true bluewater cruiser, was introduced in 1998 and remains one of the brand\u0026rsquo;s best-selling models, with nearly 1,000 boats sold.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eLagoon has always remained at the forefront of innovation, and the Lagoon 440 is the perfect example. Debuted in 2004, it had 100 orders before it had even launched. Features such as an expansive flybridge, owner\u0026rsquo;s cabin with island berth, huge windows in the hull, and a forward cockpit catapulted it into the limelight.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eCredited for its role in bringing multihulls into mainstream popularity, Lagoon has launched hybrid models such as the Lagoon 420, as well as the luxurious flagship, the Lagoon 620. The large SIXTY 5 and the eco-conscious Lagoon 51 show its diversity as a brand. The launch of SIXTY 7 and SEVENTY 8 power catamarans has opened a whole new era for Lagoon.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eLagoon has unsurprisingly been awarded a number of awards in its 40-year history, including Multihull of the Year 2023 in the sail cruising category for the Lagoon 51. Each model exudes the classic Lagoon style with a balance of strength, performance, and thoughtful design and construction. The spacious interior and deck design have made Lagoon one of the top choices for charter companies the world over, with large communal spaces, multiple cabins, and light, elegant d\u0026eacute;cor.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eIn the sailing category, the Lagoon 40, which launched in 2017, is the most compact model in the range. The new Lagoon 42 Millenium further enhances the indoor/outdoor lifestyle, with a spacious cockpit leading off the saloon and opening onto a terrace. Other sailing models include the highly capable Lagoon 43, as well as the Lagoon 46 and Lagoon 51. These models offer exceptional liveaboard experience, while retaining the ease of handling for a couple, whether they\u0026rsquo;re cruising coastally or across oceans.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe Lagoon 55 and Lagoon 60 incorporate yacht-style features, including spacious flybridges, up to 16 berths, a vast forward cockpit, and modular living spaces. The Lagoon 60 was awarded the Design Innovation Award 2024 at the Genoa Boat Show.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe semi-custom SIXTY 5 and EIGHTY 2 bring superyacht classification to Lagoon\u0026rsquo;s catamarans. These elegant, luxurious models are bound for long-haul voyages. Everything from the hull color to the interior layouts and upholstery can be customized.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eIn the power catamaran lineup, the SIXTY 7 and SEVENTY 8 are Lagoon\u0026rsquo;s first foray into this fast-emerging category. These multihull superyachts can accommodate up to 16 guests in six cabins, offering huge space thanks to the wide beam-to-length ratio. They have been awarded numerous accolades since their launches.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n&quot;,&quot;short_description&quot;:&quot;\u003cp\u003eLagoon catamarans is one of the premier brands of sailing and power catamarans in the world, with 7,000 boats built in its 40-year history. It can reach a maximum speed of over 42 knots in blissful silence. The carbon fibre construction has made it light on her feet and there is more space on-board. The most unique feature on the yacht is the \u0026#39;music hull\u0026#39;. It is located in Bejune na Gorenjskem and specialises in a wide range of sporting goods best known for their skis and snowboards. The Winter Division at Elan manufactures skis and snowboards, the Marine Division produces sailing yachts. In the year 1949, the boat building arm of the business began with the production of kayaks, canoes and small boat production made of waterproof wood. In the year 1950, with their commercial success, exporting of boats to the USA began. Elan switched its production from wood to utilise the new materials in the production of their racing kayaks and boats by the beginning of the 1960\u0026rsquo;s. It was also an advent of reinforced polyester during that period. In 1997, the Lagoon 410 became its first production volume catamaran\u0026mdash;a model remembered for its iconic and innovative vertical windows. It is a major player in the private ownership sector as well as the charter sector. Its models offer versatility, comfort, stability, and performance in equal measure.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eToday, Lagoon is a brand of Groupe Beneteau, which purchased the company in 1995. The company itself dates back to 1984, and built the first Lagoon 55 in 1987. By 1994 that lineup expanded to include five more models\u0026mdash;all built to match the high standards of race boats\u0026mdash;constructed in epoxy, glass, carbon and Kevlar. In 1997, the Lagoon 410 became its first production volume catamaran\u0026mdash;a model remembered for its iconic and innovative vertical windows. The Lagoon 380, a true bluewater cruiser, was introduced in 1998 and remains one of the brand\u0026rsquo;s best-selling models, with nearly 1,000 boats sold.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eLagoon has always remained at the forefront of innovation, and the Lagoon 440 is the perfect example. Debuted in 2004, it had 100 orders before it had even launched. The large SIXTY 5 and the eco-conscious Lagoon 51 show its diversity as a brand. The launch of SIXTY 7 and SEVENTY 8 power catamarans has opened a whole new era for Lagoon.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eLagoon has unsurprisingly been awarded a number of awards in its 40-year history, including Multihull of the Year 2023 in the sail cruising category for the Lagoon 51. Each model exudes the classic Lagoon style with a balance of strength, performance, and thoughtful design and construction. The spacious interior and deck design have made Lagoon one of the top choices for charter companies the world over, with large communal spaces, multiple cabins, and light, elegant d\u0026eacute;cor.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eIn the sailing category, the Lagoon 40, which launched in 2017, is the most compact model in the range. The new Lagoon 42 Millenium further enhances the indoor/outdoor lifestyle, with a spacious cockpit leading off the saloon and opening onto a terrace. Other sailing models include the highly capable Lagoon 43, as well as the Lagoon 46 and Lagoon 51. These models offer exceptional liveaboard experience, while retaining the ease of handling for a couple, whether they\u0026rsquo;re cruising coastally or across oceans.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe Lagoon 55 and Lagoon 60 incorporate yacht-style features, including spacious flybridges, up to 16 berths, a vast forward cockpit, and modular living spaces. The Lagoon 60 was awarded the Design Innovation Award 2024 at the Genoa Boat Show.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe semi-custom SIXTY 5 and EIGHTY 2 bring superyacht classification to Lagoon\u0026rsquo;s catamarans. These elegant, luxurious models are bound for long-haul voyages. Everything from the hull color to the interior layouts and upholstery can be customized.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eIn the power catamaran lineup, the SIXTY 7 and SEVENTY 8 are Lagoon\u0026rsquo;s first foray into this fast-emerging category. They have been awarded numerous accolades since their launches.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n&quot;,&quot;short_description&quot;:&quot;\u003cp\u003eLagoon catamarans is one of the premier brands of sailing and power catamarans in the world, with 7,000 boats built in its 40-year history. It was founded in 1989 by Henri Jeanneau as a separate brand from the well-established Jeanneau shipyard. Prestige Yachts is one of the first boatbuilders to adopt the Pod propulsion system and design a lighter, more spacious, more dependable, more comfortable yacht that has revolutionized life onboard in terms of efficiency, ease of handling, noise, and vibration.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe very first model, the Prestige 41, launched the brand, and it quickly gained a loyal following of customers. In 2000 Prestige Yachts added the first Flybridge model to its lineup, the Prestige 36 being the first of the F-Line range. It was during this time of huge expansion that the company moved to a larger facility in Les Herbiers, France, where it remains to this day.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eExpansion continued through the decades, with a dealer network established in North America, as well as the launch of the second generation F-Line including the iconic Prestige 500. New models continued to be developed over the following years, with Prestige having the largest European dealer network of any brand and over 4,000 boats sold.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe Prestige 520 was launched in 2018 on the back of the enormous success of the Prestige 500 and honored its heritage while bringing a more contemporary outlook to the model. 2020 saw the launch of the new X-Line, another big moment for the brand, with its main features being light and luxury, innovative uses of space, and a high finish.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe latest major step for Prestige is the launch of the M-Line of sleek, luxurious motor catamarans. It is a major player in this rapidly developing sector, with models such as the Prestige M48 and M8 creating villa-on-the-water style eco-yachts. These are built in Italy at the Monfalcone shipyard.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003ch2\u003eModel ranges/Models of Prestige Yachts\u003c/h2\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003ePrestige Yachts built its four ranges\u0026mdash;the F-Line, S-Line, X-Line, and M-Line\u0026mdash;over years of development and design and today offers the latest generations of these hugely popular motor yachts.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe F-Line consists of eight flybridge models ranging from the Prestige 690 down to the new F4.3. These eight mark the culmination of ideas and development of some 40 predecessors and are characterized by large windows and natural light, spacious and airy interiors, soft lines, wrap-around sea views from the owner\u0026rsquo;s suite, and cutting-edge technology.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe S-Line, consisting of the 420S, the 460S, and the 520S, bring performance, comfort, and elegance to this coupe range. Wrap-around sea views (especially from the Infinity Cockpit), huge windows, an inside/outside living space, and haute couture furnishings make these two yachts stand out in the sector. They also feature large flybridges with hard tops.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eLastly in the current lineup is the M-Line of motor catamarans. List or find bareboat, crewed, skippered Lagoon charters across the world.&quot;,&quot;master&quot;:true,&quot;approved&quot;:true,&quot;approved_by_id&quot;:null,&quot;full_description&quot;:&quot;\u003cp\u003eLagoon is one of the largest builders of multihulls in the world. It is a major player in the private ownership sector as well as the charter sector. Its models offer versatility, comfort, stability, and performance in equal measure.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eToday, Lagoon is a brand of Groupe Beneteau, which purchased the company in 1995. The company itself dates back to 1984, and built the first Lagoon 55 in 1987. By 1994 that lineup expanded to include five more models\u0026mdash;all built to match the high standards of race boats\u0026mdash;constructed in epoxy, glass, carbon and Kevlar. In 1997, the Lagoon 410 became its first production volume catamaran\u0026mdash;a model remembered for its iconic and innovative vertical windows. The Lagoon 380, a true bluewater cruiser, was introduced in 1998 and remains one of the brand\u0026rsquo;s best-selling models, with nearly 1,000 boats sold.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eLagoon has always remained at the forefront of innovation, and the Lagoon 440 is the perfect example. Debuted in 2004, it had 100 orders before it had even launched. Features such as an expansive flybridge, owner\u0026rsquo;s cabin with island berth, huge windows in the hull, and a forward cockpit catapulted it into the limelight.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eCredited for its role in bringing multihulls into mainstream popularity, Lagoon has launched hybrid models such as the Lagoon 420, as well as the luxurious flagship, the Lagoon 620. The large SIXTY 5 and the eco-conscious Lagoon 51 show its diversity as a brand. The launch of SIXTY 7 and SEVENTY 8 power catamarans has opened a whole new era for Lagoon.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eLagoon has unsurprisingly been awarded a number of awards in its 40-year history, including Multihull of the Year 2023 in the sail cruising category for the Lagoon 51. During the Multihull Boat Show 2018, the Lagoon 50 won the award of Multihull of the Year, and Lagoon SEVENTY 8 won Best Multihull Motor Yacht over 50 feet.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003ch2\u003eModel ranges/Models of Lagoon Catamarans\u003c/h2\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eLagoon has honed its lineup to offer nine sailing catamarans and two power catamarans. Each model exudes the classic Lagoon style with a balance of strength, performance, and thoughtful design and construction. The spacious interior and deck design have made Lagoon one of the top choices for charter companies the world over, with large communal spaces, multiple cabins, and light, elegant d\u0026eacute;cor.\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eIn the sailing category, the Lagoon 40, which launched in 2017, is the most compact model in the range. It was winner of the Multihull of the Year Award at the 2021 British Yachting Awards thanks to its light-filled interior, ease of handling, and cabin layout that can be customized to accommodate four to six persons.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe Lagoon 42 is one of the world\u0026rsquo;s best-selling catamarans, with over 1,000 sold to date. The new Lagoon 42 Millenium further enhances the indoor/outdoor lifestyle, with a spacious cockpit leading off the saloon and opening onto a terrace. Other sailing models include the highly capable Lagoon 43, as well as the Lagoon 46 and Lagoon 51. These models offer exceptional liveaboard experience, while retaining the ease of handling for a couple, whether they\u0026rsquo;re cruising coastally or across oceans.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe Lagoon 55 and Lagoon 60 incorporate yacht-style features, including spacious flybridges, up to 16 berths, a vast forward cockpit, and modular living spaces. The Lagoon 60 was awarded the Design Innovation Award 2024 at the Genoa Boat Show.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eThe semi-custom SIXTY 5 and EIGHTY 2 bring superyacht classification to Lagoon\u0026rsquo;s catamarans. These elegant, luxurious models are bound for long-haul voyages. Everything from the hull color to the interior layouts and upholstery can be customized.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eIn the power catamaran lineup, the SIXTY 7 and SEVENTY 8 are Lagoon\u0026rsquo;s first foray into this fast-emerging category. These multihull superyachts can accommodate up to 16 guests in six cabins, offering huge space thanks to the wide beam-to-length ratio. They have been awarded numerous accolades since their launches.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n&quot;,&quot;short_description&quot;:&quot;\u003cp\u003eLagoon catamarans is one of the premier brands of sailing and power catamarans in the world, with 7,000 boats built in its 40-year history. Its bluewater cruising cats are popular with owners and charterers thanks to their comfort, performance, safety, stability, and clever design elements.           <h2 class="flex items-center gap-3 py-5 mb-5 border-b border-b-wireframe-4 text-subtitle-3 md:text-subtitle-1">
  
            <span id="srp_info">About </span>

</h2>
          <div class="text-body-2">
            <div><p>Rightboat is a global boat marketplace connecting buyers with a wide selection of boats for sale across every major category and price range. From <a href="https://www.rightboat.com/r/day-boats-for-sale" class="text-primary-blue underline" target="_blank">small day boats</a> and <a href="https://www.rightboat.com/category/fishing-boats-for-sale" class="text-primary-blue underline" target="_blank">fishing boats</a> to cruising yachts, <a href="https://www.rightboat.com/r/power-catamarans-for-sale" class="text-primary-blue underline" target="_blank">power catamarans</a>, and <a href="https://www.rightboat.com/category/superyachts-for-sale" class="text-primary-blue underline" target="_blank">superyachts</a>, our listings cover both new and used boats from leading marine brands worldwide.</p><br><p>Buyers can explore boats for sale by type, manufacturer, length, price, year, or location. Whether you’re <a href="https://www.rightboat.com/boats-for-sale/GB" class="text-primary-blue underline" target="_blank">looking for a used boat in the UK</a>, a new power <a href="https://www.rightboat.com/boats-for-sale/US" class="text-primary-blue underline" target="_blank">boat in the USA</a>, or a sailing yacht in Europe, Rightboat makes it easy to compare options and contact sellers directly.</p><br><p>Our platform features listings from professional brokers, dealers, and manufacturers, helping you browse with confidence. Each listing includes detailed specifications, photos, and pricing to support informed buying decisions. With thousands of boats for sale added and updated regularly, Rightboat is designed to support everything from first-time boat buyers to experienced yacht owners.</p><br><p>Use the filters above to narrow your search, save your favourite listings, and sign up for alerts when new boats matching your criteria are listed. Whether you’re buying locally or internationally, Rightboat helps simplify the process of finding the right boat.</p><br><p> </p><br><h2 class="text-subtitle-2">Buy New and Used Boats with Confidence</h2>

<p>Buying a boat is a big decision, and Rightboat is designed to make that process simpler and more transparent. Our boats for sale include both new and used listings from verified brokers, dealers, and manufacturers, giving buyers access to accurate information, competitive pricing, and a wide range of options.</p><br><p>Whether you are upgrading to a larger yacht, purchasing your first boat, or searching for a specific make or model, Rightboat allows you to explore listings in one place and contact sellers directly. With boats listed from countries around the world, you can compare local and international options side by side.</p><br><p> </p><br><h2 class="text-subtitle-2">Boat Types Available on Rightboat</h2>

<p>Rightboat features boats for sale across all major boating categories. From practical day boats to long-range cruising yachts, our platform supports every type of boating lifestyle.</p><br><p>Popular boat types include <a href="https://www.rightboat.com/category/power-for-sale" class="text-primary-blue underline" target="_blank">power boats for speed and versatility</a>, <a href="https://www.rightboat.com/category/sail-for-sale" class="text-primary-blue underline" target="_blank">sailboats for relaxed cruising</a>, catamarans for stability and space, and motor yachts for comfort and long-distance travel. You will also find specialist listings such as fishing boats, trawlers, RIBs, and superyachts.</p><br><p> </p><br><h2 class="text-subtitle-2">Browse Boats for Sale by Location</h2>

<p>Looking for a boat in a specific country or region? Rightboat makes it easy to browse boats for sale by location, helping you find listings near you or in popular boating destinations.</p><br><p>Buyers regularly search for boats for sale in the United Kingdom, United States, Europe, and the Mediterranean, but our listings extend worldwide. Filtering by location allows you to consider factors such as transport, import regulations, and local boating conditions when comparing listings.</p><br><p> </p><br><h2 class="text-subtitle-2">Popular Boat Categories on Rightboat</h2>

    <h2 class="flex items-center gap-3 py-5 mb-5 border-b border-b-wireframe-4 text-subtitle-3 md:text-subtitle-1">
  
       FAQs

          <div class="py-8 border-b border-b-wireframe-4">
  <div data-hidden-content="#faq_1016" class="flex items-center justify-between w-full cursor-pointer">
    <p class="font-bold text-body-1 text-black">What types of boats can I find on Rightboat?</p>
    <i class="fa-solid fa-angle-down fa-lg"></i>
  </div>
   <div class="hidden" id="faq_1016"> <div><p>Rightboat features a wide range of boats for sale, including power boats, sailboats, catamarans, motor yachts, fishing boats, RIBs, and superyachts. Listings include both new and used boats from sellers worldwide.</p>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="py-8 border-b border-b-wireframe-4">
  <div data-hidden-content="#faq_1017" class="flex items-center justify-between w-full cursor-pointer">
    <p class="font-bold text-body-1 text-black">Are the boats for sale on Rightboat new or used?</p>
    <i class="fa-solid fa-angle-down fa-lg"></i>
  </div>
   <div class="hidden" id="faq_1017"> <div><p>Rightboat lists both new and used boats for sale. You can filter results by condition to view only new boats, only used boats, or a combination of both depending on your preference.</p>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="py-8 border-b border-b-wireframe-4">
  <div data-hidden-content="#faq_1018" class="flex items-center justify-between w-full cursor-pointer">
    <p class="font-bold text-body-1 text-black">Can I search for boats for sale in a specific country or location?</p>
    <i class="fa-solid fa-angle-down fa-lg"></i>
  </div>
   <div class="hidden" id="faq_1018"> <div><p>Yes. Rightboat allows you to browse boats for sale by country or location. This makes it easy to find boats near you or explore listings in popular boating regions around the world.</p>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="py-8 border-b border-b-wireframe-4">
  <div data-hidden-content="#faq_1019" class="flex items-center justify-between w-full cursor-pointer">
    <p class="font-bold text-body-1 text-black">Who lists boats for sale on Rightboat?</p>
    <i class="fa-solid fa-angle-down fa-lg"></i>
  </div>
   <div class="hidden" id="faq_1019"> <div><p>Boats on Rightboat are listed by professional brokers, dealers, and manufacturers. This helps ensure accurate listings, detailed specifications, and reliable seller information to support confident buying decisions.</p>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="py-8 border-b border-b-wireframe-4">
  <div data-hidden-content="#faq_1020" class="flex items-center justify-between w-full cursor-pointer">
    <p class="font-bold text-body-1 text-black">Can I compare different boats before contacting a seller?</p>
    <i class="fa-solid fa-angle-down fa-lg"></i>
  </div>
   <div class="hidden" id="faq_1020"> <div><p>Yes. Rightboat’s search tools and filters allow you to compare boats by price, size, year, manufacturer, and location so you can narrow down options before contacting sellers directly.</p>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="py-8 border-b border-b-wireframe-4">
  <div data-hidden-content="#faq_1021" class="flex items-center justify-between w-full cursor-pointer">

    <i class="fa-solid fa-angle-down fa-lg"></i>
  </div>
   <div class="hidden" id="faq_1021"> <div><p>Yes. Rightboat features international boat listings, allowing buyers to explore boats for sale across multiple countries. Many buyers use Rightboat to compare local and international options before purchasing.</p>

<div class="py-8 border-b border-b-wireframe-4">
  <div data-hidden-content="#faq_1022" class="flex items-center justify-between w-full cursor-pointer">

    <i class="fa-solid fa-angle-down fa-lg"></i>
  </div>
   <div class="hidden" id="faq_1022"> <div><p>Boat prices vary widely depending on the type, size, age, and condition. On Rightboat, you can find smaller used boats at entry-level prices, while larger motor yachts, catamarans, and luxury yachts can cost significantly more. Using filters for price, boat type, and condition helps buyers quickly find options within their budget.</p>
